 1
 Things can be improved if job design, workplace design and workflow are correct
 iske saath hi yah bhi dhyaan rakhen ki kisi bhi emploi ke upar kaam kaa jarurat se zyada vajan na ho

 2

 aapako emploij kii jimmedaari or bhoomika spasht kerani chahie

 4
 company ko emploij ko is tarah se saport karnaa chahie ki unke work-life balance main sudhaar ho

 5

 Generally, we all know that eating sprouted grains is beneficial, but what are its benefits, less people will know
 ankurit anaaj khaane ke phaayde:1
 You must have heard that breakfast in the morning should be heavy and healthy
 aise main ankurit anaaj kaa seven karnaa ek bahut acha vikalp he
 If you wish, you can change the type of cereal everyday
 isse aapako vairieti bhi milti rahegi
 People usually eat only sprouted with moong spider and gram, but you can soak soybean someday if you want
 ye sabhi anaaj protein or duusare poshak tatwon se bharpoor hote hai
 In such a situation, it is very good to take it in breakfast in the morning
 2
 Sprouted grains help the digestive system to remain strong and active
 isamen fibre kii bahut adhik maatra hoti he jo pachan kriya ko sahi banaae rakhti he
 3
 ankurit anaaj main kai tarah ke poshak tatv paae jate hai
 It is rich in anti-oxidants and vitamins A, B, c and E
 anti-oxident kii vajah se rog-pratirohak kshamta behatar hoti he, vahiin isamen maujuud lavan sharir kii duusari aavashyakton ko bhi puraa karte hai
 It contains major salts such as phosphorus, iron, calcium, zinc and magnesium
 4
 Many types of proteins are found in sprouted grains, due to which the body gets strength and the muscles also become strong
 5
 Sprouted grains contain a very small amount of calories

 Know 10 special things about this practice of Jainism
 1
 Jainism has two sects, Shvetambara and Digambara

 5
 jain dharm main santhara kii ginati kisi upwas main nahin hoti

 santhara kii shuruyaat sabase pehle suryoday ke baad 48 minute takaupavasase hoti he, jisamen vyakti kuch peetaa bhi nahin he
 This fast is called Naukarthi
 7
 Fasting in Santhara can be done both with and without drinking water
 8
 Before taking Santhara, it is necessary to take the permission of family and guru
 9
 It is a tradition to voluntarily give up the body
